CREATE TABLE  `game_transaction_turnover_report` (
  `GAME_TURNOVER_REPORT_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `SHAN_GAME_TRANSACTION_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `GAME_TRANSACTION_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0',
  `GAME_ID` varchar(64) CHARACTER SET utf8 NOT NULL,
  `TOTAL_GAME_PLAYS` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `TOTAL_STAKE` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `TOTAL_WIN` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `RAKE_PERCENTAGE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `TOTAL_RAKE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `TOTAL_MARGIN` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `TOTAL_NET` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PARTNER_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `CREATED_DATE` datetime NOT NULL,
  `UPDATED_DATE` date NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`GAME_TURNOVER_REPORT_ID`),
  UNIQUE KEY `UNIQUE_INDEX_GAME_ID` (`GAME_ID`,`UPDATED_DATE`),
  KEY `FK_game_transaction_turnover_report_1` (`PARTNER_ID`),
  KEY `COMP_IND_CREATED_DATE_PARTNER_ID_` (`CREATED_DATE`,`PARTNER_ID`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_game_transaction_turnover_report_1` FOREIGN KEY (`PARTNER_ID`) REFERENCES `partner` (`PARTNER_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

CREATE TABLE  `hand_history` (
  `HAND_HISTORY_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `PLAY_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `USER_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `PLAY_GROUP_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `TOURNAMENT_ID` bigint(100) NOT NULL,
  `TOURNAMENT_TABLE_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `INTERNAL_REFERENCE_NO` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `GAME_REFERENCE_NO` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `STAKE` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `WIN` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `REVENUE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `RAKE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `POT_AMOUNT` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `TABLE_CARD` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `PLAYER_CARD` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `PLAYER_INDEX` bigint(5) DEFAULT '0',
  `WIN_TYPE` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `WIN_RESULT_TYPE` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `WIN_HANDS` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `USER_DETAILS` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL,
  `RANK_HOLDER` bigint(5) DEFAULT '0',
  `USER_HAND` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `USER_ORDERS` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `WINNER_MAP` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PRE_FLOP` varchar(1000) DEFAULT NULL,
  `FLOP` varchar(1000) DEFAULT NULL,
  `TURN` varchar(1000) DEFAULT NULL,
  `RIVER` varchar(1000) DEFAULT NULL,
  `CREATED_DATE` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `CUSTOM1` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `CUSTOM2` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `CUSTOM3` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `CUSTOM4` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `CUSTOM5` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,

  `CUSTOM7` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `CUSTOM8` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `CUSTOM9` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `CUSTOM10` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`HAND_HISTORY_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

CREATE TABLE  `role` (
  `ROLE_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `ROLE_NAME` varchar(150) NOT NULL,
  `FK_ROLE_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `ROLE_DESC` text NOT NULL,
  `STATUS` int(1) NOT NULL,
  `ONLINE_AGENT_STATUS` int(3) DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'onlie 0,agent 1',
  `MENU_ORDER` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `LINK` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `CREATED_BY` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `CREATED_DATE` datetime NOT NULL,
  `UPDATED_BY` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  `UPDATED_DATE` datetime NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`ROLE_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

CREATE TABLE  `role_to_admin` (
  `ROLE_TO_ADMIN_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `FK_ROLE_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `FK_ADMIN_USER_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `CREATE_DATE` datetime NOT NULL,
  `CREATE_BY` varchar(64) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`ROLE_TO_ADMIN_ID`),
  KEY `FK_role_to_admin_1` (`FK_ROLE_ID`),
  KEY `FK_role_to_admin_2` (`FK_ADMIN_USER_ID`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_role_to_admin_1` FOREIGN KEY (`FK_ROLE_ID`) REFERENCES `role` (`ROLE_ID`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_role_to_admin_2` FOREIGN KEY (`FK_ADMIN_USER_ID`) REFERENCES `admin_user` (`ADMIN_USER_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

  `MASTER_TRANSACTTION_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `FK_PARTNER_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `FK_BALANCE_TYPE_ID` int(3) NOT NULL,
  `FK_TRANSACTION_STATUS_ID` int(3) NOT NULL,
  `FK_TRANSACTION_TYPE_ID` int(3) NOT NULL,
  `TRANSACTION_AMOUNT` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `TRANSACTION_DATE` datetime NOT NULL,
  `INTERNAL_REFERENCE_NO` varchar(32) NOT NULL,
  `CURRENT_TOT_BALANCE` decimal(20,2) NOT NULL,
  `CLOSING_TOT_BALANCE` decimal(20,2) NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`MASTER_TRANSACTTION_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

CREATE TABLE  `user_turnover_report_daily` (
  `USER_TURNOVER_REPORT_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `USER_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `GAME_TRANSACTION_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `PARTNER_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `GAME_ID` varchar(65) NOT NULL,
  `TOTAL_BETS` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `TOTAL_WINS` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `NET` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `REPORT_DATE` datetime NOT NULL,
  `UPDATED_DATE` date NOT NULL,

  UNIQUE KEY `UNIQUE_KEY_USER_ID_DATE` (`USER_ID`,`GAME_ID`,`UPDATED_DATE`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

  `PARTNER_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,

) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=1 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

1. UPDATE user set ONLINE_AGENT_STATUS=1; ->this is to update the online status

set fk_partner_type_id=0 for admin
2. UPDATE partner SET FK_PARTNER_TYPE_ID=CASE WHEN IS_OWN_PARTNER=1 THEN 11 WHEN IS_DISTRIBUTOR=1 THEN 12
WHEN IS_SUBDISTRIBUTOR=1 THEN 13 ELSE 14 END; ->this is to update, whether the partner is a dis or subdist or an agent using IS_DIST,IS_SUBDIST columns

3. need to add all the data from partner to admin_user table
INSERT INTO admin_user(USERNAME,FIRSTNAME,PASSWORD,FK_PARTNER_ID,EMAIL,ACCOUNT_STATUS,ONLINE_AGENT_STATUS)
SELECT PARTNER_USERNAME,PARTNER_NAME,PARTNER_PASSWORD,PARTNER_ID,PARTNER_EMAIL,1,1 FROM partner WHERE PARTNER_ID=125;

4. need to add data in role and role_to_admin table based on the user(agent,distributor or subdist)
SET FOREIGN_KEY_CHECKS = 0; execute the below query through putty
INSERT INTO role_to_admin(fk_role_id,fk_admin_user_id,create_date,create_by)
SELECT role_id,1,NOW(),'admin' from role where status=1; //it should be done to every user like magent, admin

CREATE TABLE  `yagent_game_turn_over_history` (
  `AGENT_GAME_TURN_OVER_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `GAME_TRANSACTION_ID` bigint(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `USER_ID` bigint(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PARTNER_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `PARTNER_NAME` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `SUBDISTRIBUTOR_ID` bigint(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `SUBDISTRIBUTOR_NAME` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `DISTRIBUTOR_ID` bigint(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `DISTRIBUTOR_NAME` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MAIN_AGEN_ID` bigint(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MAIN_AGEN_NAME` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `GAME_ID` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `GAME_NAME` varchar(70) DEFAULT NULL,
  `GAME_DESCRIPTION` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `TOTAL_GAME_PLAYED` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PLAY_POINTS` decimal(20,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `WIN_POINTS` decimal(20,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MARGIN` decimal(20,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `NET` decimal(20,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MARGIN_PERCENTAGE` decimal(20,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PARTNER_COMMISSION_TYPE` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `START_TIME` datetime NOT NULL,
  `END_TIME` datetime NOT NULL,
  `CREATED_ON` date NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`AGENT_GAME_TURN_OVER_ID`),
  UNIQUE KEY `UNIQUE_KEY` (`USER_ID`,`CREATED_ON`,`GAME_ID`,`GAME_DESCRIPTION`),
  KEY `FK_yagent_game_turn_over_history_2` (`PARTNER_ID`),
  KEY `COMP_IND_USER_ID_GAME_ID_CREATED_ON` (`USER_ID`,`GAME_ID`,`GAME_DESCRIPTION`,`CREATED_ON`),
  KEY `INDEX4_GAME_TRANSACTION_ID` (`GAME_TRANSACTION_ID`),
  KEY `COMP_INDEX_SUBDISTRIBUTOR_ID` (`SUBDISTRIBUTOR_ID`,`START_TIME`),
  KEY `COMP_INDEX_DISTRIBUTOR_ID` (`DISTRIBUTOR_ID`,`START_TIME`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_yagent_game_turn_over_history_1` FOREIGN KEY (`USER_ID`) REFERENCES `user` (`USER_ID`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_yagent_game_turn_over_history_2` FOREIGN KEY (`PARTNER_ID`) REFERENCES `partner` (`PARTNER_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

CREATE TABLE  `ydistributor_game_turn_over_history` (
  `DISTRIBUTOR_GAME_TURN_OVER_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `GAME_TRANSACTION_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `USER_ID` bigint(50) NOT NULL,
  `PARTNER_ID` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PARTNER_NAME` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `SUBDISTRIBUTOR_ID` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `SUBDISTRIBUTOR_NAME` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `DISTRIBUTOR_ID` bigint(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `DISTRIBUTOR_NAME` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MAIN_AGEN_ID` bigint(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MAIN_AGEN_NAME` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `GAME_ID` varchar(100) NOT NULL,
  `GAME_NAME` varchar(70) DEFAULT NULL,
  `GAME_DESCRIPTION` varchar(70) DEFAULT NULL,
  `TOTAL_GAME_PLAYED` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PLAY_POINTS` decimal(20,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `WIN_POINTS` decimal(20,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MARGIN` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `NET` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MARGIN_PERCENTAGE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PARTNER_COMMISSION_TYPE` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL,
  `START_TIME` datetime NOT NULL,
  `END_TIME` datetime NOT NULL,
  `CREATED_ON` date NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`DISTRIBUTOR_GAME_TURN_OVER_ID`),
  UNIQUE KEY `UNIQUE_KEY` (`USER_ID`,`GAME_ID`,`GAME_DESCRIPTION`,`CREATED_ON`),
  KEY `FK_ydistributor_game_turn_over_history_2` (`DISTRIBUTOR_ID`),
  KEY `COMP_INDEX_USER_ID__GAME_ID_CREATED_ON` (`USER_ID`,`GAME_ID`,`GAME_DESCRIPTION`,`CREATED_ON`),
  KEY `INDEX3_GAME_TRANSACTION_ID` (`GAME_TRANSACTION_ID`),
  KEY `COMP_INDEX_DISTRIBUTOR_ID` (`DISTRIBUTOR_ID`,`START_TIME`),
  KEY `COMP_INDEX_MAIN_AGEN_ID` (`MAIN_AGEN_ID`,`START_TIME`,`GAME_DESCRIPTION`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_ydistributor_game_turn_over_history_1` FOREIGN KEY (`USER_ID`) REFERENCES `user` (`USER_ID`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_ydistributor_game_turn_over_history_2` FOREIGN KEY (`DISTRIBUTOR_ID`) REFERENCES `partner` (`PARTNER_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

CREATE TABLE  `yuser_turnover_history` (
  `USER_TURN_OVER_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `USER_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `GAME_TRANSACTION_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `USER_NAME` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PARTNER_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `PARTNER_NAME` varchar(50) NOT NULL,
  `SUBDISTRIBUTOR_ID` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `SUBDISTRIBUTOR_NAME` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `DISTRIBUTOR_ID` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `DISTRIBUTOR_NAME` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MAIN_AGEN_ID` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MAIN_AGEN_NAME` varchar(50) DEFAULT NULL,
  `GAME_ID` varchar(70) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MINIGAMES_ID` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `GAME_DESCRIPTION` varchar(70) DEFAULT NULL,
  `TOTAL_GAME_PLAYED` bigint(20) DEFAULT NULL,
  `TOTAL_BETS` decimal(20,2) NOT NULL,
  `TOTAL_WINS` decimal(20,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `TOTAL_NET` decimal(20,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PARTNER_COMMISSION_TYPE` int(10) NOT NULL,
  `SUBDIST_PARTNER_COMMISSION` int(3) DEFAULT NULL,
  `DIST_PARTNER_COMMISSION` int(3) DEFAULT NULL,
  `MAIN_AGENT_COMMISSION_TYPE` int(3) DEFAULT NULL,
  `PARTNER_REVENUE_SHARE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `SUBDISTRIBUTOR_REVENUE_SHARE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `DISTRIBUTOR_REVENUE_SHARE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `MAIN_AGNET_REVENUE_SHARE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `GAME_REVENUE_SHARE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `SUBDIS_GAME_REVENUE_SHARE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `DIST_GAME_REVENUE_SHARE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00',
  `MAIN_AGNET_GAME_REVENUE_SHARE` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `START_TIME` datetime NOT NULL,
  `END_TIME` datetime NOT NULL,
  `CREATED_ON` date NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`USER_TURN_OVER_ID`),
  UNIQUE KEY `COMP_INDEX_USER_ID_GAME_ID_DATE` (`USER_ID`,`GAME_ID`,`GAME_DESCRIPTION`,`CREATED_ON`) USING BTREE,
  KEY `FK_yuser_turnover_history_2` (`PARTNER_ID`),
  KEY `COMP_INDEX_SUBDISTRIBUTOR_ID` (`SUBDISTRIBUTOR_ID`,`GAME_TRANSACTION_ID`),
  KEY `INDEX_GAME_TRANSACTION_ID` (`GAME_TRANSACTION_ID`),
  KEY `COMP_INDEX_USER_ID_DATE` (`USER_ID`,`MINIGAMES_ID`,`CREATED_ON`),
  KEY `COMP_SUBDISTRIBUTOR_ID_GAME_ID` (`SUBDISTRIBUTOR_ID`,`GAME_ID`),
  KEY `COMP_DISTRIBUTOR_ID_GAME_ID` (`DISTRIBUTOR_ID`,`GAME_ID`),
  KEY `COMP_MAIN_AGEN_ID_GAME_ID` (`MAIN_AGEN_ID`,`GAME_ID`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_yuser_turnover_history_1` FOREIGN KEY (`USER_ID`) REFERENCES `user` (`USER_ID`),
  CONSTRAINT `FK_yuser_turnover_history_2` FOREIGN KEY (`PARTNER_ID`) REFERENCES `partner` (`PARTNER_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;

CREATE TABLE `group_mp_sub_menu_info` (
  `GRP_MP_SM_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `PARTNER_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `GROUP_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `SUB_MENU_ID` bigint(20) NOT NULL,
  `CREATE_BY` varchar(64) DEFAULT NULL,
  `CREATE_DATE` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`GRP_MP_SM_ID`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=44476 DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;


UPDATE coin_type SET NAME='REAL_CASH',VALUE=0,DESCRIPTION='Play With Real Cash' WHERE COIN_TYPE_ID=1;
UPDATE coin_type SET STATUS=0 WHERE COIN_TYPE_ID IN(2,3);

UPDATE user_points SET coin_type_id=1;

UPDATE partner SET FK_PARTNER_ID=1 WHERE FK_PARTNER_TYPE_ID=11;

ALTER TABLE adjustment_transaction ADD COLUMN COIN_TYPE_ID INTEGER DEFAULT 1 AFTER ADJUSTMENT_COMMENT;

ALTER TABLE adjustment_transaction MODIFY COLUMN INTERNAL_REFERENCE_NO VARCHAR(64);
ALTER TABLE partner_adjustment_transaction MODIFY COLUMN INTERNAL_REFERENCE_NO VARCHAR(64);
ALTER TABLE user ADD COLUMN LIVE_CASINO INT(1) DEFAULT 0 AFTER MOBILE_LOGIN_STATUS;

delete from role_to_admin where role_to_admin_id=38;

ALTER TABLE `user` MODIFY COLUMN `ONLINE_AGENT_STATUS` INT(5) DEFAULT 1;
